About the plane one: Clearly Magneton! Has electric attacks (super effective against steel/flying planes), but even better can levitate to plane-height, use thunder wave to paralyse the planes, and then use the magnet pull ability to gently lower the planes down so that the people inside are safe. Maybe you would need a few Magnetons, since each Magnetons can only take one plane, but that is still the best mon by far. Early enough (gen 1, gen 2 for electric/steel type). Note that magneton can levitate, although it doesn't have the ability in-game; the mon is two generations older than the ability and the anime has clearly shown that its prior evolution can levitate, and several Dex entries clearly state it as well.
